      :ARG0 (u / university :name (n / name :op1 "HKUST"))
      :ARG1 (a / and
            :op1 (t / technology
                  :mod (n2 / new))
            :op2 (p / product
                  :mod n2)
            :quant (m / more-than :op1 30)
            :ARG0-of (c / cover-01
                  :ARG1 (r / range
                        :mod (w / wide)
                        :mod (t2 / technology)
                        :ARG2-of (i / include-91
                              :ARG1 (a2 / and
                                    :op1 (n3 / nanotechnology)
                                    :op2 (m2 / multimedia)
                                    :op3 (l / logistics)
                                    :op4 (t3 / technology :name (n4 / name :op1 "RFID"))
                                    :op5 (m3 / manufacture-01
                                          :mod (a3 / advance))
                                    :op6 (b / biotechnology)))))))

# ::id PROXY_XIN_ENG_20041219_0059.16 ::date 2013-08-11T11:58:09 ::snt-type body ::annotator SDL-AMR-09 ::preferred
# ::snt HKUST also collaborated with a prominent mainland manufacturer on the development of a nanomaterial-based high-capacity lithium battery.
# ::save-date Sun Aug 11, 2013 ::file PROXY_XIN_ENG_20041219_0059_16.txt
(c / collaborate-01
      :ARG0 (u / university :name (n / name :op1 "HKUST"))
      :ARG1 (c2 / company
            :ARG0-of (m / manufacture-01)
            :mod (p / prominence)
            :location (m2 / mainland))
      :ARG2 (d / develop-02
            :ARG1 (b / battery
                  :consist-of (l / lithium)
                  :mod (b2 / base-02
                        :ARG1 b
                        :ARG2 (n2 / nanomaterial))
                  :mod (c3 / capacity
                        :mod (h / high))))
      :mod (a / also))

# ::id PROXY_XIN_ENG_20041219_0059.17 ::date 2013-08-11T13:22:34 ::snt-type body ::annotator SDL-AMR-09 ::preferred
# ::snt This collaboration is the most recent in a series of successful technology transfer agreements reached by HKUST.
# ::save-date Sun Aug 11, 2013 ::file PROXY_XIN_ENG_20041219_0059_17.txt
(c / collaborate-01
      :mod (t / this)
      :time (r / recent
            :degree (m / most))
      :ARG1-of (i / include-91
            :ARG2 (s / series
                  :mod (a / agreement
                        :mod (t2 / transfer-01
                              :ARG1 (t3 / technology))
                        :mod (s2 / successful)
                        :ARG1-of (r2 / reach-01
                              :ARG0 (u / university :name (n / name :op1 "HKUST")))))))

# ::id PROXY_XIN_ENG_20041219_0059.19 ::date 2013-08-11T09:49:59 ::snt-type body ::annotator SDL-AMR-09 ::preferred

# ::save-date Sun Aug 11, 2013 ::file PROXY_XIN_ENG_20041219_0059_19.txt
(i / increase-01
      :ARG0 (u / university :name (n / name :op1 "HKUST"))
      :ARG1 (f / fund-01
            :ARG1 (r / research-01
                  :ARG1 (t / technology
                        :ARG1-of (r2 / require-01
                              :ARG0 (i2 / industry
                                    :location (c / country-region :name (n2 / name :op1 "Pearl" :op2 "River" :op3 "Delta"))))
                        :mod (n3 / new)))))

# ::id PROXY_XIN_ENG_20041219_0059.20 ::date 2013-08-11T09:53:24 ::snt-type body ::annotator SDL-AMR-09 ::preferred
# ::snt The University will continue to leverage its extensive relationships with international research institutions and multi-national corporations to enhance the development of advanced technologies which can find immediate practical application in China.
# ::save-date Tue Aug 20, 2013 ::file PROXY_XIN_ENG_20041219_0059_20.txt
(c / continue-01
      :ARG0 (u / university)
      :ARG1 (l / leverage-01
            :ARG0 u
            :ARG1 (r / relationship
                  :mod (e / extensive)
                  :prep-with (a / and
                        :op1 (i2 / institution
                              :mod (i3 / international)
                              :mod (r2 / research-01))
                        :op2 (c2 / corporation
                              :mod (m / multi-national)))
                  :poss u)
            :purpose (e2 / enhance-01
                  :ARG0 u
                  :ARG1 (d / develop-02
                        :ARG1 (t / technology
                              :mod (a2 / advance)
                              :mod (p / possible
                                    :domain (f / find-01
                                          :ARG1 (a3 / application
                                                :mod (i4 / immediate)
                                                :mod (p2 / practical)
                                                :location (c3 / country :name (n / name :op1 "China"))))))))))
